09/08/24, 12:39â€¯am - Jamesy: #include <simplecpp>
main_program{
    turtleSim();
    int x;
    int y;
    int z;
    cin>>x;
    cin>>y;
    z=(500-x*y)/(x-1); //z=spacing b/w squares
    repeat(x) {repeat(x) {repeat(4) {forward(y);right(90);}}
    penUp();
    forward(z+y);
    penDown();}  // made the whole row
    penUp();
    forward(-x*(z+y)); //came back
    right(90); forward(y+z); right(-90);
    penDown();}
    hide(true);
    wait(30);
}

13/08/24, 10:08â€¯pm - Yogesh Sangwan: #include <simplecpp>
main_program{
    int n;
    int j=1;
    cin>>n;
    for(int i=1;i<=((2*n)-1);i=i+2){
        repeat(n-j){
            cout<<" ";
        }
        repeat(i){
            cout<<"* ";

        }
        repeat(n-j){
            cout<<" ";
        }
        j=j+1;
        cout<<endl;
    }
    for(int i=2*n-3;i>=1;i=i-2){
        j=j-1;
        repeat(n-j+1){
            cout<<" ";
        }
        repeat(i){
            cout<<"* ";

        }
        repeat(n-j+1){
            cout<<" ";
            
        }
        cout<<endl;
    }
    for(int i=3;i<=n;i=i+2){
        repeat(n-j){
            cout<<" ";
        }
        repeat(i){
            cout<<"* ";

        }
        repeat(n-j){
            cout<<" ";
        }
        j=j+1;
        cout<<endl;
    }

}

20/08/24, 10:23â€¯pm - Jamesy: #include <simplecpp>
main_program{
    int sum1=0, t1, n, d1=1, p, sum2=0, d2=1, t2, z, x, y;
    z=0;
    cin>>n>>p;
    {while(n>1)
    { t1=n%2;
    sum1=sum1 + t1*d1;
    n=n/2;
    d1=d1*10;
    }
    if(n==1)
    {
        sum1=sum1+d1;
    }
    }// this is the whole code for converting a integer number to binary number and that binary number is 'sum'

     {while(p>1)
    { t2=p%2;
    sum2=sum2 + t2*d2;
    p=p/2;
    d2=d2*10;
    }
    if(p==1)
    {
        sum2=sum2+d2;
    }
    }
     
     while(sum1>0 || sum2>0)
     {
        x=sum1%10;
        y=sum2%10;
        if(x!=y)
        {z++;}
        sum1=sum1/10;
        sum2=sum2/10;
     }

cout<<z;
}

27/08/24, 10:02â€¯pm - Yogesh Sangwan: #include<simplecpp>
int ctz(int n){
        int i=0,p=1;
        if(n>0 && n<=1000){
        while(p<=n){
                int t=p;
        while (t%5==0){
                t/=5;
                i++;}
                p++;
        }
        }
        else cout<< "not possible";
        return i;
}
main_program{
        int n;
        cin >>n;
        cout << ctz(n) << endl;
}

void countTrailingZeros(int n)
{int t,sum=0,x=5;
   while(x<=n) {t=n/x;
    sum=sum+t;
    x=x*5;}
    cout<<sum;

}

    cin>>p;
    countTrailingZeros(p);
}

01/09/24, 12:20â€¯pm - Jamesy: #include <simplecpp>

int sumOfDigits( long long int n)
{int sum=0,t;
    while(n>0)
    {t=n%10;
    sum=sum+t;
    n=n/10;
    }
    return sum;
}

int numberOfIterations(long long int m)
{
   int sum,x,t,count=0;
   x=m;
   do
   {sum=0;
           if(m<10) break;
     while(x>0)
    {t=x%10;
    sum=sum+t;
    x=x/10;
    }
    count++;

    x=sum;
   }
    while(sum>=10);
    return count;
}

void printIterations(int m)
{
    int sum,x,t,count=0;
   x=m;
   do
   {sum=0;
     while(x>0)
    {t=x%10;
    sum=sum+t;
    x=x/10;
    }
    count++;

    x=sum;
   if(count>=2) cout<<sum<<" ";
   }
    while(sum>=10);

}



main_program{
   long long int j;
    cin>>j;
    cout<<numberOfIterations(j)<<endl;
    cout<<sumOfDigits(j)<<" ";
    printIterations(j);
}

29/10/24, 9:47â€¯pm - Yogesh Sangwan: #include "matrix.h"

void add(matrix<int> & A, matrix<int> & B, matrix<int> & C){
    for(int i = 0 ; i < A.rows(); i++){
        for(int j = 0 ; j < A.cols(); j++){
            C[i][j] = A[i][j] + B[i][j];
        }
    }
}

void multiply(matrix<int> & A, matrix<int> & B, matrix<int> & C){
    for(int i = 0 ; i < A.rows(); i++){
        for(int j = 0 ; j < A.cols(); j++){

            int row = i;
            int col = j;

            int s = 0;
            for(int k = 0 ; k < A.rows(); k++){
                s  += A[row][k]*B[k][col];
            }

            C[i][j] = s;
        }
    }
}
29/10/24, 9:47â€¯pm - Yogesh Sangwan: #include <iostream>
#include "rental.h"
#include <iomanip>

Car::Car(std::string modelName, std::string licensePlate, float rentalRate){
    this -> modelName = modelName;
    this -> licensePlate = licensePlate;
    this -> rentalRate = rentalRate;
}

void Rental::addCar(const Car &car){
    cars.push_back(car);
}

void Rental::rentCar(const string & licensePlate, int numberOfDays){
    Car c;
    for(auto i: cars){
        if(i.licensePlate == licensePlate){
            c = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    displayRentalDetails(c, this -> calculateRentalCost(c.rentalRate, numberOfDays));
}
void Rental::displayRentalDetails(const Car & car, float totalCost){
    std::cout << "Car Model: " << car.modelName << std::endl;
    std::cout << "License Plate: " << car.licensePlate << std::endl;
    std::cout << std::fixed << std::setprecision(2) << "Total Rental Cost: $" << totalCost << std::endl;
}

float Rental::calculateRentalCost(float rentalRate, int numberOfDays){
    return (rentalRate*numberOfDays);
}

09/07/25, 4:08â€¯pm - Jamesy: Y - yaar things aren't working for me anymore, I don't have interest for my work.. kya karu
J - interest was a fluke
Y - what? mera passion hai DASH m and I want to follow that professionally
J - passion is nothing 
Y - kya bol raha hai.. bachpan se meri hobby thi DASH karna and I always loved that, so what's wrong with that
J - ye sab alag hai, don't confuse them
Y - confuse what
J - interest, hobby, passion.. you developed interest in DASH just because you first tried that and were slightly better than others around, got praised, thought to invest time in it
Y - is that a wrong thing?
J - no, depends on the wise choice of what you invested
Y - invested what
J - time... pass-time or the valuable
Y - what
J - investing your pass-time gives rise to promoting your interest to hobby, in which you are not actually good but do for relaxation.. investing your valuable time actually makes you good at something, which after gaining your interest, come to be known as passion
Y - isn't this how you find your passion?
J - well, how can you call it 'your passion' if it isn't unique..
Y - NOT UNIQUEEE, why so
J - see perseverance is what it takes, your ability to finish work through tough situations.. assume you have 100 coins and have 5 jars in front of you, you decide how much to invest in which.. if you invest more in a jar you become better in that field, investing in other will make you higher in another aspect.. its the level of perseverance you put in one to become better in that..
Y - how isn't passion unique then?
J - passion is a subset of hobby, which all started from promoting interest.. if the 'idea of having interest' was itself surrounding and time dependant then how could you trust the fluked base.. the process is reproducible
Y - then if no one will have liking for their work then how will everything work?
J - well, world runs on perseverance, not on passion. every work has its beauty and motivation to do which eventually creates liking, affected by external biasness we just don't prefer some of them
Y - external biasness?
J - stereotypes, money, peer pressure and all
Y - then a person becoming an engineer suddenly changes field to singing and becomes a famous singer, isn't that the his passion which awakened?
J - things demand tolerance levels which are filled by persons perseverance.. a person complete work A can also complete work B if the tolerance level demand for 'A' is higher than B which is lower or equal to person's tolerance level.. perseverance power increases with time and efforts one puts
Y - then why don't everybody becomes good in everything in their tolerance range if that's the case..
J - it requires time and people generally don't want to change the investment stocks in which they already invested much and go back to square to start entirely different set of investment.. the one's who do, makes a tough choice which people turn out to confuse with passion.. people like to invest in the things they already had some background of, which connects back to their unplanned stocks of hobby and choosing one for passion
Y - so you are saying that I should continue my thing and shouldn't change to DASH?
J - no, just make a wise choice.. not based all the crap floating

14/07/25, 9:27â€¯pm - Yogesh Sangwan: I worked onto a small idea of simplifying taxi experience and booking for BITS pilani students. Growing up near BITS Pilani I saw how overpriced the local taxi options were especially with no Uber available. Drawing from my familiarity with the campus and leveraging my uncleâ€™s two taxis, I launched a small initiative to streamline the booking experience for BITS students. I collected data on pricing, car types, and space requirements, and designed a simple service card under our names. Sharing it through my network within BITS, the idea gained initial traction. However, I soon faced real-world challenges like disagreements over pricing onto my discount ideas and the importance of maintaining clear communication and professional boundaries with other drivers too. This experience gave me a practical taste of entrepreneurship and taught me valuable lessons about execution, negotiation, and relationship management. Maybe this ENT course will get me correct upon those mistakes.

4. Preventing Schedule Clashes

5. Extra Help Sessions

I will strive to remain approachable and honest, keeping you informed about every step and welcoming your input throughout the year.

%%%%%%% Command Subsection Headers %%%%%%%
\renewcommand{\subsection}[4]{
	\def\temp{#4}
	\vspace{2pt}
	{
		\large
		{\color{violet} \textbf{#1}} | {\sl \color{Green} #2} \filldate{#3}
		\ifx\temp\empty
		\else
		{
			\\[0.1em]
			\fontsize{11}{13.2}\selectfont
			\sl #4
		}
		\fi
	}
}

\section{Key Projects}

\subsection{Predator-Prey Model}{LearnerSpace}{May 2025 - Jul 2025}{Electrical, IIT Bombay}
\begin{itemize}
    \item Designed and simulated an \textbf{analog computer} architecture in \textbf{LTspice} to model Lotkaâ€“Volterra predatorâ€“prey dynamics using multipliers,weighted op-amp summers, and \textbf{Howland integrators}
    \item Implemented nonlinear population interaction through \textbf{hardware-level multiplication} and differential equations
    \item Validated oscillatory preyâ€“predator cycles via \textbf{parameter scaling}, ensuring \textbf{analog stability} and accurate emulation of biological systems
\end{itemize}

\subsection{Combinatorial and Sequential Circuits}{Digital Circuits Laboratory}{Jul 2025 - Present}{Under Prof. Saurabh Lodha, Department of Electrical Engineering, IIT Bombay}
\begin{itemize}
    \item Learnt implementation of Structural, Behavioural, and Dataflow Modelling on Quartus to build logic circuits
    \item Constructed various logic gates, multiple bit Full Adders, Multipliers, Arithmetic Logic Units, Multiplexers, Encoders,
Shifters, BCD-Adders, Sequential logic circuits and Sequence generators using a\textbf{ Finite State Machine(FSM)}
    \item Implemented the circuits on an \textbf{XEN10} board using \textbf{FPGAs} and used \textbf{ScanChain} for hardware verification
\end{itemize}

\subsection{Quadcopter Design and Implementation}{Course Project : Makerspace}{Jan 2025 - Apr 2025}{Under Prof. Joseph John}
\begin{itemize}
    \item  Gained knowledge in \textbf{quadcopter dynamics} and\textbf{ control theory}, implementing a \textbf{PID controller} for stabilization
    \item Assembled a \textbf{quadcopter} from scratch, integrating components like the \textbf{ESP32, Arduino,} and various sensors \textbf{(IMU, GPS)} with\textbf{ PID }controller, allowing it to be controlled via a mobile app via WiFi joystick input
    \item Applied principles of \textbf{mechatronics} and systems integration to successfully combine hardware (ESP32, Arduino, sensors) and software components into a functional, single-purpose robotic system
\end{itemize}

	{
		\large

		\else
		{
			\\[0.1em]
			\fontsize{11}{13.2}\selectfont
			\sl #4
		}
		\fi
	}
}

My name is Manan, a Chemical Engineering undergraduate at IIT Bombay, currently moving into my third year. While I value the technical discipline my core field has taught me, Iâ€™m deeply drawn to finance for its dynamic blend of structured problem-solving and market understanding.


Iâ€™m reaching out to express my interest in contributing to a research project in the finance/economics domain. I believe this will help me build a strong foundation in market analysis, investment decision-making, and financial modeling-skills I wish to strengthen before stepping into high-stakes finance roles. A research setting, under experienced mentorship, offers the ideal opportunity to do this meaningfully.


I have demonstrated strong research and analytical skills through various projects. In ConsultX, I led the research on overcrowding in Mumbai local trains, using issue trees and guesstimates to structure the problem. I worked with regression, KNN, and XGBoost models to analyze commuter data and forecast passenger load patterns.
In a Venture Capital Case Competition, I evaluated the financials and market potential of a hypothetical company, Urban Ease, conducting extensive market research, competitive analysis, and financial modeling to assess its investment viability. Moreover, I have also previously interned in a VC, where I worked first-hand on valuation techniques and market research to make investment decisions.

I have also previously done a Finance project revolving around using Reinforcement Learning models to optimize stock trading. Even though I thoroughly enjoyed working on the project, it lacked structure because it was a project led by a few senior students and so the learning outcome was not as high. Thank you for your time and consideration.
